\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Each pair of functions are called before (enter function) and after (leave) a type M\+PI call. Which pair depends on the type of the call, and the functions called are E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+P\+Y\+\_\+$<$call$>$\+\_\+enter and leave.
